     <h1 class="pg-headline">

     </h1>

        <section class="zn zn-body-text zn-body zn--idx-0 zn-has-multiple-containers zn-has-18-containers" data-containers="18" data-eq-pts="xsmall: 0, medium: 460, large: 780, full16x9: 1100" data-vr-zone="zone-1-0" data-zn-id="body-text" id="body-text">
         <div class="l-container">
          <div class="el__leafmedia el__leafmedia--storyhighlights el__leafmedia--">
           <div class="el__storyhighlights_wrapper">
            <div class="el__storyhighlights">
             <h3 class="el__headline">
              Story highlights
             </h3>
             <ul class="el__storyhighlights__list">
              <li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">
               In exchange, the government will drop charges against arrested protesters
              </li>
              <li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">
               Ukraine is mired in a political crisis that has led to the Prime Minister's resignation
              </li>
              <li class="el__storyhighlights__item el__storyhighlights--normal">
               The opposition wants more concessions from the government
              </li>
             </ul>
            </div>
            <div class="ad ad--epic" data-ad-text="show">
             <div class="ad-ad_ns_btf_01" id="ad_ns_btf_01">
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Ukrainian protesters vacated the capital's city hall Sunday in exchange for the government dropping charges against arrested demonstrators, an official said.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Protesters vacated city hall, unblocked a major street and left other government buildings as part of an amnesty deal calling for the opposition to vacate government buildings in Kiev, opposition parliament member Arsen Avakov said.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           They had occupied the city hall for nearly three months.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Protesters will remain outside city hall and will not allow police inside, he said. The opposition plans to hold a rally Sunday morning.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Ukraine is mired in a political crisis that has led to the Prime Minister's resignation.
          </p>

typeof cvp.reportAnalytics === 'function') {if (prevVideoId.length === 0 &amp;&amp; document.referrer &amp;&amp; document.referrer.search(/\/videos\//) &gt;= 0) {prevVideoId = document.referrer.replace(/^(?:http|https)\:\/\/[^\/]\/videos\/(.+\.\w+)(?:\/video\/playlists\/.*)?$/, '/video/$1');if (prevVideoId === document.referrer) {prevVideoId = '';}}cvp.reportAnalytics('videoPageData', {videoCollection: currentVideoCollectionId,videoBranding: CNN.omniture.branding_content_page,templateType: CNN.omniture.template_type,nextVideo: nextVideoId,previousVideo: prevVideoId,referrerType: '',referrerUrl: document.referrer});}},onContentBegin: function (containerId, cvpId, contentId) {/** Before the video ad starts, the freewheel companion ad* html needs to be placed on the page so that it can be* triggered by Freewheel to display the companion ad.* onContentBegin triggers updateCompanionLayout which* handles the logic to switch from epic to companion ads* with the 'removeEpicAds' layout*/if (CNN.companion &amp;&amp; typeof CNN.companion.updateCompanionLayout === 'function') {CNN.companion.updateCompanionLayout('removeEpicAds');}clearTimeout(moveToNextTimeout);CNN.VideoSourceUtils.clearSource(containerId);},onContentComplete: function (containerId, cvpId, contentId) {/** When the video is completely done then restore the* freewheel tag to the page. The epic tags were already* added to the page when the video content began playing* after the ad played using the onContentPlay event.*/if (CNN.companion &amp;&amp; typeof CNN.companion.updateCompanionLayout === 'function') {CNN.companion.updateCompanionLayout('restoreFreewheel');}navigateToNextVideo(contentId, containerId);},onContentEnd: function (containerId, cvpId, contentId) {/* Add a VisualRevenue event on video end */if (Array.isArray(window._vrq)) {window._vrq.push(['video', 'stop', configObj.video]);}}};if (typeof configObj.context === 'undefined' || configObj.context === null) {configObj.context = 'europe'.replace(/[\(\)-]/g, '');}if (CNN.VideoPlayer.apiInitialized) {window.cnnVideoManager.renderMultipleContainers({videoConfig:configObj, eventsCallback:callbackObj});} else {CNN.VideoPlayer.addVideo(configObj, callbackObj);}});
           </script>

          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Thousands of demonstrators have packed Kiev's Independence Square since November, when President Viktor Yanukovych reversed a decision to sign a trade deal with the European Union and instead turned toward Russia.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Violent confrontations flared after a sweeping anti-protest law was signed weeks ago, and an uneasy standoff remains on the streets.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Despite concessions such as the deal, Ukraine's opposition parties continue to call for constitutional reforms to shift power away from the president.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Ukraine, a country of 45 million people, is split between pro-European regions in the West and a more Russia-oriented East.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Its leader and Russian President Vladimir Putin agreed on a $15 billion deal for Russia to buy Ukrainian debt and slash the price of natural gas.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">
           Yanukovych has resisted calls for him to step down and defended the government's handling of the political crisis.
          </p>
          <p class="zn-body__paragraph">

Lugansk, a separatist held city close to the border with Russia, has witnessed some of the heaviest fighting between Russian backed separatist soldiers and Ukrainian troops. A lack of electricity, food, fuel and water are making life difficult for the remaining residents of the city. Despite a declared ceasefire between separatists forces and the Ukrainian military, tensions on the ground are still high throughout the east of the country. Sporadic shelling is heard in Donetsk daily and gunfire in the port city of Mariupol. The city of Donetsk has only around 300,000 people remaining out of a population of 900,000 due to the fighting. (Photo by Spencer Platt/Getty Images)" class="media__image media__image--responsive" data-demand-load="not-loaded" data-eq-pts="mini: 0,  xsmall: 221,  small: 308,  medium: 461,  large:  781" data-src-full16x9="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140920134854-russia-convoy-ukraine-horizontal-large-gallery.jpg" data-src-large="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140920134854-russia-convoy-ukraine-horizontal-large-gallery.jpg" data-src-medium="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140920134854-russia-convoy-ukraine-horizontal-large-gallery.jpg" data-src-mini="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140920134854-russia-convoy-ukraine-hp-video.jpg" data-src-mini1x1="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140920134854-russia-convoy-ukraine-topics.jpg" data-src-small="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140920134854-russia-convoy-ukraine-story-top.jpg" data-src-xsmall="http://i2.cdn.turner.com/cnnnext/dam/assets/140920134854-russia-convoy-ukraine-story-body.jpg" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhEAAJAJEAAAAAAP///////wAAACH5BAEAAAIALAAAAAAQAAkAAAIKlI+py+0Po5yUFQA7"/>
